Required for the rules API\n    98→\ts.HTTP.UseEncodedPath()\n    99→\n   100→\tvar sourceIPs *middleware.SourceIPExtractor\n   101→\tif serverCfg.LogSourceIPs {\n   102→\t\tvar err error\n   103→\t\tsourceIPs, err = middleware.NewSourceIPs(serverCfg.LogSourceIPsHeader, serverCfg.LogSourceIPsRegex, serverCfg.LogSourceIPsFull)\n   104→\t\tif err != nil {\n   105→\t\t\t// This should have already been caught in the Server creation\n   106→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   107→\t\t}\n   108→\t}\n   109→\n   110→\tapi := &API{\n   111→\t\tcfg:            cfg,\n   112→\t\tAuthMiddleware: cfg.HTTPAuthMiddleware,\n   113→\t\tserver:         s,\n   114→\t\tlogger:         logger,\n   115→\t\tsourceIPs:      sourceIPs,\n   116→\t\tindexPage:      newIndexPageContent(serverCfg.PathPrefix),\n   117→\t}\n   118→\n   119→\t// If no authentication middleware is present in the config, use the default authentication middleware.\n   120→\tif api.AuthMiddleware == nil {\n   121→\t\tapi.AuthMiddleware = middleware.AuthenticateUser\n   122→\t}\n   123→\n   124→\t// Unconditionally add middleware that ensures we only accept requests with an expected number of tenants\n   125→\t// that is applied after any existing auth middleware has run. Only a single tenant is allowed when federation\n   126→\t// is disabled. If federation is enabled, there is optionally a max number of tenants that is supported.\n   127→\tapi.AuthMiddleware = middleware.Merge(api.AuthMiddleware, newTenantValidationMiddleware(federationCfg.Enabled, federationCfg.MaxTenants))\n   128→\n   129→\treturn api, nil\n   130→}\n   131→\n   132→// RegisterDeprecatedRoute behaves in a similar way to RegisterRoute. RegisterDeprecatedRoute also logs warnings on\n   133→// invocations of the deprecated endpoints.\n   134→func (a *API) RegisterDeprecatedRoute(path string, handler http.Handler, auth, gzipEnabled bool, method string, methods ...string) {\n   135→\tmethods = append([]string{method}, methods...)\n   136→\thandler = a.deprecatedHandler(handler)\n   137→\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering deprecated route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"path\", path, \"auth\", auth, \"gzip\", gzipEnabled)\n   138→\ta.newRoute(path, handler, false, auth, gzipEnabled, methods...)\n   139→}\n   140→\n   141→func (a *API) deprecatedHandler(next http.Handler) http.Handler {\n   142→\tl := util_log.NewRateLimitedLogger(time.Minute, a.logger, time.Now)\n   143→\n   144→\treturn http.HandlerFunc(func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n   145→\t\tlevel.Warn(l).Log(\"msg\", \"api: received a request on a deprecated endpoint\", \"path\", r.URL.Path, \"method\", r.Method)\n   146→\t\tnext.ServeHTTP(w, r)\n   147→\t})\n   148→}\n   149→\n   150→// RegisterRoute registers a single route enforcing HTTP methods. A single\n   151→// route is expected to be specific about which HTTP methods are supported.\n   152→func (a *API) RegisterRoute(path string, handler http.Handler, auth, gzipEnabled bool, method string, methods ...string) {\n   153→\tmethods = append([]string{method}, methods...)\n   154→\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"path\", path, \"auth\", auth, \"gzip\", gzipEnabled)\n   155→\ta.newRoute(path, handler, false, auth, gzipEnabled, methods...)\n   156→}\n   157→\n   158→func (a *API) RegisterRoutesWithPrefix(prefix string, handler http.Handler, auth, gzipEnabled bool, methods ...string) {\n   159→\tlevel.Debug(a.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"api: registering route\", \"methods\", strings.Join(methods, \",\"), \"prefix\", prefix, \"auth\", auth, \"gzip\", gzipEnabled)\n   160→\ta.newRoute(prefix, handler, true, auth, gzipEnabled, methods...)\n   161→}\n   162→\n   163→func (a *API) newRoute(path string, handler http.Handler, isPrefix, auth, gzip bool, methods ...string) (route *mux.Route) {\n   164→\t// Propagate the consistency level on all HTTP routes.\n   165→\t// They are not used everywhere, but for consistency and less surprise it's added everywhere.\n   166→\thandler = propagation.Middleware(&querierapi.ConsistencyExtractor{}).Wrap(handler)\n   167→\n   168→\tif auth {\n   169→\t\thandler = a.AuthMiddleware.Wrap(handler)\n   170→\t}\n   171→\tif gzip {\n   172→\t\thandler = gziphandler.GzipHandler(handler)\n   173→\t}\n   174→\tif isPrefix {\n   175→\t\troute = a.server.HTTP.PathPrefix(path)\n   176→\t} else {\n   177→\t\troute = a.server.HTTP.Path(path)\n   178→\t}\n   179→\tif len(methods) > 0 {\n   180→\t\troute = route.Methods(methods...)\n   181→\t}\n   182→\troute = route.Handler(handler)\n   183→\n   184→\treturn route\n   185→}\n   186→\n   187→// RegisterAlertmanager registers endpoints that are associated with the alertmanager.\n   188→func (a
